1a1(1): srid pa rgya mtsho bzhi'i rgyud ces bya ba bzhugs so//
1b1(1): rgya gar skad du/ du ra ka pi tan+ta/ bod skad du/ srid pa rgya mtsho bzhi'i rgyud ces bya ba/ yab mngon rdzogs rgyal po dang / yum rigs pa'i rgyal mo la phyag 'tshal lo// 'das
1b2(1): dang ma 'ongs kyi mtshams su/ 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ gser gyi nyi ma'i gdan la/ rig pa'i ye shes gzhal yas 'bar ba ru/ ye shes rang snang gdal ba la/
1b3(1): rigs lnga'i sangs rgyas kyi khri la/ sku ru bla med khrag 'thung brjid pa/ mnga' dbang lhun gyis rdzogs pa/ mdzad pa gar gyi phyag rgyas bzhugs te/ brtul shugs chen po'i mnga' bdag
1b4(1): bum pa'i 'khor lo la rin po che'i 'od 'bar ba/ pad+ma'i lce la zangs kyi mu khyud 'khyil pa/ gser gyi 'khor lo la mu tig gi 'bur 'phang bcas pa/ srid pa'i sa gzhi la mu tig gi
2a1(1): shar bu 'phro ba/ bdud rtsi'i thig le hUM bcur 'bar ba/ tshon sbrel bzhi la hUM bzhi brten pa/ chags pa'i 'dab ma la b+ha ru'i hUM bcu 'bar ba/ rna ba ya hUM bzhis 'brel
2a2(1): ba/ gser gyi 'khor lo la shel gyi hUM bcu 'bar ba/ 'bur bzhi hUM bzhis bsrung ba/ chags pa sna tshogs rigs la mu khyud mu tig gi hUM bcus la 'khrigs pa las/ zhug pa bzhi la
2a3(1): hUM bzhis mdzes pa/ yum gyi mkha' lnga dbu ma la phrin las bzhi'i dkyil 'khor chags pa/ dbus rdo rje dbyings ma la rgya bzhi'i lcags dang ldan te sangs rgyas thams cad bskyed pa'i
2a4(1): za ma tog tu gnas so// rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rwa lnga las/ byang chub sems lnga'i char bzhugs pa'i gnas 'dzin pa'i gnas bzhir bab pa/ de lta bu'i yum la sku las hUM bdun ha lnga
2b1(1): muM gcig tu shar te/ thugs las hUM muM gnyis/ muM bzhi hUM mtshan gsum du ldan te/ yon tan las b+h+yo lnga bcu drug tu shar ba/ ru mtshon bzhi la b+h+yo bzhi/ b+ha ga bzhi la hUM bzhi/ de lta bu'i yab yum la/ sku'i spyi
2b2(1): dpal gyi khro bo bcu la ta kr-ita bzhis bskor ba dang / gsung gsang chen gyi khro bo bcu la ta krita bzhis bskor ba dang / thugs gdeng chen gyi khro bo bcu la ta kr-ita bzhis bskor ba/ yon tan rdzogs chen gyi khro bo
2b3(1): bcu la ta kr-ita bzhis bskor bas/ de lta bu'i yab yum la dkar mo'i mdo bcu gsum dang / nag mo'i mdo bco brgyad dang / ser mo'i mdo lnga bcu drug dang / sprul pa'i ma mo brgyad du ldan te thabs cig tu
2b4(1): bzhugs so// de nas srid pa'i phra men rgya mtshos 'di skad ces gsol to// yab yum srid pa'i bca' bzhi kun// gtan tshigs rtsa ba ji ltar lags// rdzogs sangs rgyas la bdag nyan 'tshal// yang dag rdzogs
2b5(1): kyis bka' stsal pa// phra men rgya mtsho gsang ba'i yum// gtan tshigs rtsa ba 'di rnams kun// srid pa'i rtsa ba mtsho bzhir bshad// phra men rgya mtshos yang gsol pa// srid pa'i rtsa ba mtsho bzhi ji ltar
2b6(1): lags// mngon rdzogs yab kyis bka' stsal pa// mtsho bzhi srid pa'i don bshad pa// srid pa'i bya lud rgya mtsho dang // dbang phyug las kyi rgya mtsho dang // bskang lung las kyi rgya mtsho dang // brtan ma las kyi rgyu
3a1(1): mtsho rnams// yang dag nyid du bshad par bya'o// ma mo srid pa'i rgya mtsho bzhi las/ gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// // bya lung srid pa'i rgya mtsho las// dang po bcas dang gnyis pa
3a2(1): skongs// gsum pa dgra yi bye brag go/ srid pa'i ma mo thams cad dang // pho yi rigs su gtogs pa kun// srid pa 'khrug pa'i byad bstan pa// nam mkha' smug nag 'thibs pa la// dred mo ral pa 'dzings pa
3a3(1): byung // de ni ma mo 'khrug pa'i byad// gnam la seng ge dkar mo dang // 'brug ris sngon mo 'thab pa'i rtags// sa la gnam lcags 'bar ba'i 'khrug/ glang po rba la mchongs pa yis// sa la stag seng 'dzings
3a4(1): pa byung // gnam la sprin dmar mched pa yis// sa la bud med ral 'dzings byung // skar mda' nam mkhar 'phros pa yis// sa la dbyig gi nor bu nyams// ri rab rtse la me chen 'bar// sa la lci ba'i zas
3a5(1): rnams za// rgya mtsho'i gting nas sbrul gdug langs// sa la me tog bcud dang bral// mkha' la stag mo mchongs pa de// sa la rnal 'byor rdzi bas bskyed// mkha' la bya rgod sder chen 'dzings// sa la gter gyi
3a6(1): bcud nyams 'gyur// g.yu sha dkar mo ra 'dzings pas// sa la dus kyi do ba 'byung // tho rangs seng ge ngu zhing 'bod// sa la rno dpal ngar du 'bab// srod la gser gyi sbud pa spud// sa la rma bya g.yengs par
3b1(1): 'gyur// g.yu sgong sngon mo gnam du yar// lcags kyi ser ba thab tu 'bab// shel dkar nang du dug gis bkang // zangs sgong dmar po zur du 'dril// mi bzad 'bar ba klad la bskor// mi bzad 'bar
3b2(1): ba'i nad zer 'byung // nyi ma sprin gyi shugs can 'khrugs// tshub ma dmar po nam mkhar 'phyo// seng ge gangs kyi stod nas lhung // sgo nas shel gyi sgo nga yar// nam mkha'i dkyil nas sprin chen ral// sa la bong
3b3(1): bu'i bcud chen zags// bse skong khra bo rgya mtshor 'bar// sa la lcug phran zor gyi 'debs// gza' skar 'khrug pa'i cho 'phrul ni// zo ba rgyan gyi rtse mo ru// za 'og sbud lhub min nam pa chags pa ni// de la
3b4(1): ltas ngan dgra bzlog bya// srid pa mtsho bzhi las/ ltas ngan gyi dgra ji ltar 'byung ba'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// // phra men rgya mtshos yang gsol pa// bcas kyi rim pa ci ltar lags// rdzogs sangs rgyas la
3b5(1): bdag nyan 'tshal// rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi bka' stsal pa// sa yi 'khor lo sbyangs pa la// 'og gzhi rus sbal khog pa la// gser gyi 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad la// gling bzhi 'khor yug gling phran ldan// mtha'
3b6(1): ma lcags ri nag po la// rin chen sna lnga'i gcal bkram ste// rtsibs brgyad steng du klu brgyad bri// 'bru sna lnga yi ngar phye la// zhabs brgyad klu brgyad brdzis par bya// zhabs kyi rtse ni phyi ru bstan// zhabs
4a1(1): brgyad bang rim mtha' mas btegs// bang rim lte ba'i pho brang la// dbus su chags 'dzin chen mo la// bud med lnga bcu lnga yis bskor// rdo rje'i ka ba bzhi yis btegs// de steng bang rim par
4a2(1): ma la// dbus su phra men rgya mtsho la// bud med bcu bdun 'khor gyis bskor// rdo rje'i ka ba bzhi yis btegs// de steng bang rim gsum pa la// bum pa zhal lnga'i dbyibs su bya// nang gi dbus su dgod pa
4a3(1): ni// dbus su srid pa'i rgyal mo la/ dbyings kyi ma bdun 'byung lnga'i yum// bcu gnyis yang dag dkyil 'khor ldan// mtshams dang yan lag ma klu yang chen brgyad// dang po dung sgong bcu gsum la// mtshal
4a4(1): gyis kha mig gshag pa bri// dbus kyi bum pa nyid la'o// spyan gzigs gtor ma phra men snod// kha khyer dang po 'khor bar bzhag/ dar dkar ru mtshon bcu gsum gzug/ thugs kyi bang rim pho brang
4a5(1): la// lcags sgong nag po bco brgyad dang // dar nag ru mtshon bco brgyad gzug/ spyan gzigs gtor mas 'khor bar bya// yon tan bang rim pho brang la// bsre sgong khra bo lnga bcu drug/ dar ser ru mtshon de
4a6(1): bzhin bya// rgyan gyi gtor ma dgram par bya// yan lag bzhi dang b+ha ga bzhi// sgo nga brgyad dang ru mtshon brgyad// de bzhin gnas su dgod par bya// phyi khyams mda' bzhi me long bzhi// ral gri bzhi dang gur
4b1(1): du bcas// gcig gis gzugs med dngos su bskang // srid pa mtsho bzhi las bcas kyi le'u ste gsum pa'o// // phra men rgya mtshos yang gsol pa// bskang gi rim pa gang lags pa// rdzogs sangs
4b2(1): rgyas la bdag nyan 'tshal// yang dag rdzogs kyis bka' stsal pa// hUM/ dung mkhar zo ba'i nang shed nas// srid pa'i rgyal mo yum gcig ma// dkar mo mdzes ma shel ltar dag/ sman gyi ga'u bu mang
4b3(1): 'dzin// spyan nas zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'char// thugs las me long ye shes gsal// mi bskyod dbyings nas thugs rje gsal// nam mkha'i mdangs la khyab pa mo// 'gro ba yongs kyi mdangs 'phrog ma// hUM/
4b4(1): yum chen dbu las sprul pa ni// dung sgong 'bar ba dkar po gcig/ mtho ste nam mkha'i dbyings su 'bar// dma' ste rgya mtsho'i gting na nyal// lcags kyi sgo nga rang rdol bas// rigs su sbrum thun mchu zlum
4b5(1): byung // de nas rigs kyi mig dkar ba// rma bya'i bu mo ha lo mgrin// dpral ba'i dkyil na zla gam ni// ri rab kyi zom dang mnyam/ kha dog sna tshogs ni// bder gshegs kyi rigs dang mnyam// spyan mig ni
4b6(1): dmar bzlog pas/ khams gsum ni dbang du sdud// 'phrag le ni g.yas gong nas// ri rab ni gong ltar 'phen// 'phrag le ni g.yon gong nas// rgya mtsho ni zho ltar bshig/ g.yu sder 'bar ba
5a1(1): yis// 'gro drug ni gnas nas 'dren// g.yas kyi 'dab gshog bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis kyis// sangs rgyas bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis rol pa mdzad// g.yon gyi 'dab gshog drug cu rtsa brgyad la// ma mo
5a2(1): drug cu rtsa brgyad rol pa mdzad// bskang ngo srid pa'i rgyal mo'i thugs dam bskang // mi la ni srid pa med// bya la ni srid pa yod// mi la ni mtho 'jung med// bya la ni mtho 'jung yod// mi yi glud du bya ba zhes
5a3(1): shig/ gser mkhar ga'u 'bar ba nas// dkar mo'i rgyal mo mi bzad ma// 'bar ma glog gi bang ba can// gser gyi dril zhags sdog cing 'phen// mi 'gyur dbyings nas 'od gsal ma// bya thang dkar ni ga
5a4(1): yang zhu ni// mthing nag nam mkha'i na bza' la// gzha' tshon 'bar ba'i mtha' chag can// 'di yi mdangs kyis thugs dam bskang // gti mug nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// rnal 'byor nyams pa skong gyur
5a5(1): cig/ g.yu sgong kha 'bar nang nas ni// sngon mo g.yu yi 'phur rtsal can// mthing nag nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan can// nyi zer zhags pas skye 'gro 'dren// bya sbyin dkar ni g.yang zhu ni// na bza' mthing nag na
5a6(1): bza' la// nyi zer dmar po'i 'od kyis mdzes// ljags la glog dmar lams se lam// 'di yi mdangs kyis bskang byas pas// gti mug nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// dam tshig nyams pa skong gyur
5b1(1): cig/ zangs mkhar dmar po 'bar ba na// dmar mo khrag gi pho 'thing can// sprin dmar mched pa'i na bza' can// byu ru'i zhags pas 'gro ba 'dren// bya lcog 'bar ba'i gyur mo mgrin// chos kyi sgra sgrogs
5b2(1): nam mkha'i dbyings su khyab// the brang gnyis las shar ba'i sras gcig ma// mthun pa'i rdzas chen 'di yis skong // gti mug nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// dam tshig nyams pa skong gyur cig/ shel mkhar 'od
5b3(1): gsal mdzes pa na// spyan ni zla tshes 'bar ba la// zhal ni g.yu zhal sngon mo ste// g.yu yi smin ma lams se lam// zla tshes zhags pa sdog cing 'phen// mkha' la rgyu ba'i ma mo ste// thugs rje dbyings nas rol
5b4(1): pa mdzad// rig byed gsal ba'i thang dkar ni// zla ba tshes gcig dbu la rdzogs// spyan ni khro chu 'bar ba la// na bza' shel dkar mdzes pas brgyan// rig pa 'di yis thugs dam bskang // mu men mdzes
5b5(1): pa'i dkyil 'khor nas// mthing nag nam mkha'i go zu la// rdo rje ha yi cha ga can// spu gri 'bar ba lag na thogs// so sor rtog pa'i thugs mnga' ba// tshul khrims ldan pa'i rig pa can// bcos kyi ras ka sku
5b6(1): la gsol// gzi yi phreng bas dbu la mdzes// rig byed 'di yi mdangs kyis bskang // gti mug nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// gser mkhar gru bzhi ldem pa na// ser mo rlung gi go zu can// rdo rje
6a1(1): rgya gram phra bkye ba// 'dzum pa'i mdangs kyis srid pa gsal// 'dre bya rig byed mdangs ldan ma// zangs kyi zhabs mas lus mdzes shing // 'di yi mdangs kyis bskang byas pas// ma rig nad
6a2(1): rnams byang bar mdzod// rlung gi dkyil 'khor zla gam nas// lag na ba dan lce brgyad thogs// bsam pa tsam gyis phyogs bcur phyin// srog chags kun gyi dbugs la nyul// 'od ldan bkrag gsal rlung
6a3(1): bzhon ma// s+phu ru rgyal mtshan mdzes ldan 'bar// lus la bra pha ma tsa ra yang ma ra tsas brgyan// 'di yi mdangs kyis bskang byas pas// ma rig nad rnams byang bar mdzod// hUM/ nam mkha' yangs pa'i dkyil
6a4(1): 'khor nas// skye med 'gro ba bkrag gi bdag/ seng ge'i gdangs skad phyogs bcur sgrogs// zhe sdang nad rnams bzhi par mdzod// seng ge dkar mo'i mdangs kyis bskang // g.yu bya khrag mig mdangs kyis
6a5(1): bskang // sems kyi nad rnams byang bar mdzod// byang phyogs rlung gi dkyil 'khor nas// ljang mo steng gsum khyab par 'gro// khyung gi skad kyis klu bdud 'joms// phrag dog nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// bya khyud
6a6(1): sngon mo'i mdangs kyis bskang / kha rlangs nam mkha' sprin du 'khrigs// rlabs kyis nam mkha' khebs par gcod// 'di yi mdangs kyis bskang byas pas// ma rig nad rnams byang bar mdzod// rgya mtsho chen
6b1(1): po'i dkyil 'khor nas// dmar mo chu yi 'khor lo can/ khrag gi ral pas stong gsum khebs// 'dod chags nad rnams byang bar mdzod// dud kha 'bar ba'i mdangs kyis bskang // ma rig nad rnams byang bar
6b2(1): mdzod// me ri gru gsum 'bar ba nas// me yi 'od las sprul pa mo// ral pa me stag me dpung 'bar// glang chen mdangs kyis gshin rje 'joms// nga rgyal nad rnams byang bar mdzod// glang chen gzugs kyi
6b3(1): rgyal pos bskang // ma rig nad rnams byang bar mdzod// gser gyi sa gzhi 'bar ba nas// ser mo rdo rje'i ral pa can// lag na sa yi dkyil 'khor thogs// gti mug nad rnams byang bar mdzod// mi yi rgyal
6b4(1): mtshan 'bar bas bskang // ma rig nad rnams byang bar mdzod// dkar mo'i rgyal mo blon mo dang // bar mtshams blon mo gong ler bcas// dung sgong dkar mo bcu gsum la// mtshal gyi thig phran 'bar bas
6b5(1): brgyan// dkar mo'i tshogs kyi thugs dam bskang // bskang bzlog chen mo'i dus la bab// dar gyi ru mtshon 'bar ba 'dis// dpung bzhi'i tshogs kyi dpung chen bzlog/ thugs dam chen po skong gyur cig/ dus
6b6(1): bzhi dpal gyi gtor ma yis// dbyings kyi ma bdun dus kyi sring // thugs dam chen po skong gyur cig/ dkar mo sgeg la thugs dam dbyings gyi lha// mdog bzang dbyings kyi yum chen la sogs
7a1(1): rnams// thugs rje'i dbyings nas shar ba'i grub pa mo// mi 'gyur chos kyi dbyings las phyi rol med// thugs rje mi 'gyur dbyings nas sku sprul pa// gang zag shes bya'i bag chags ci mchis
7a2(1): pa// byams mgon khyod kyi spyan sngar mthol zhing bshags/ khyed kyi thugs rje nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam// 'gro ba kun la snyoms pa'i thugs rje can// rtog med thugs dam rang gi dgongs nas kyang // nyon
7a3(1): mongs sgrib pa ma lus sbyang du gsol// srid pa'i las kyis mnar ba'i sems can rnams// dang po ma rig 'khor ba'i gnas la 'khyams// byams mgon thugs rjes dgongs nas sbrang du gsol// dkar mo
7a4(1): 'od gsal srid pa'i rgyal mo dang // dbyings kyi ma bdun dus kyi sring mo lnga// mthun pa'i rdzas dang mchod pa'i yo byad rnams// bsgrub pa'i dus su gnas su bstab byas na// dam skong phrin las chen po mdzad du
7a5(1): gsol// dkar mo gshog thogs nam mkhar 'phur pa'i tshogs/ brtson 'grus mthar phyin phyi bshol mi mnga' bas// 'gro drug thugs rjes gnas nas drang du gsol// sems can las kyi bag chags dbang
7a6(1): gis na// dam tshig chen po'i bskang bzlog 'di byas pas// srid pa'i dgra ltas ngan pa bzlog tu gsol// srid pa mtsho bzhi las/ dkar mo'i mdos kyi skong / bya lung las kyi rgya mtsho las/ dkar mo'i mdos
7b1(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // phra men rgya mtshos yang gsol pa// nag mo'i rim pa gang lags pa// rdzogs sangs rgyas la bdag nyan 'tshal// spyi dpal chen pos bka' stsal pa// hUM/ yum gyi thugs
7b2(1): mchog 'bar ba las// gser kyi thig le gru gsum nas// btso ma gser gyi skrag pa la// rdo rje ha yi phreng bas brgyan// thugs las ye shes 'od gsal ma/ khyod kyi thugs dam bskang ba ni// lcags sgong nag po
7b3(1): 'bar ba la// g.yu yi thig phran 'bar ba 'phros// yum gyi thugs las sprul pa ste// mtho yang de ni mi mtho ste// ri rab kyi ni zom las 'phar// dma' yang de ni mi dma' ste// rgya mtsho chen po'i gting nas
7b4(1): nyul// sgo nga rang gis rang brdol bas// sha zan mchu gug rigs su byung // bya chen 'di yi dpral ba ni// ri rab 'bum pa'i gtos dang mnyam// dbu la g.yu yi ra 'bar ba// nam mkha'i khams kyi mthongs su
7b5(1): slebs/ kha yis klu bdud dregs pa ni// 'og gi rgya mtsho'i gting nas 'dren// mig ni nyi zla 'bar ba ste// klu brgyad zil gyis gnon par byed/ kha nas me 'bar rgya mtsho skems// sems ni chags sdang lnga dang
7b6(1): ldan// sder mo g.yu sder 'bar ba yis// chu srin nag po'i snying nas 'dren/ kha rlangs na bun bzhin du chags// dung gi gshog 'dab 'bar bar ba las// g.yu yi gshog rtse zer 'phro bas// thags bzangs
8a1(1): ris kyi mgo bo gcod// g.yas kyi gshog pa brkyang ba yis// lha yi dbang po'i gnas la khyab// g.yon gyi gshog pa rlabs pa yis// gser gyi sa gzhi 'bar ba gshog/ lto nas 'brug sngon
8a2(1): 'bar ba 'khrug kha nas glog 'khyug ldibs se ldib// lce yi rtse las thog chen 'bebs// mig nas lcags kyi ser chen 'bebs// sna nas bu yug tshub mar 'tshubs/ khyod kyi tsit+ta 'bar ba nas// zur phud lnga
8a3(1): pa'i cho 'phrul 'gyed// mkhal ma ag ni de ba ste// mchin pa ro gling chen po la// mkhris pa gsod byed chen po ste// mcher pa myos byed 'bar ba la// glo ba skyod byed stobs can te// grod pa sde dpon chen po
8a4(1): ste// gnye ma dbang ldan 'bar bar sprul// sgal tshigs 'khor lo bcu drug la// srid pa'i pho rgyud bcu drug sbrul// g.yas kyi gshog sbubs lnga bcu drug khrag 'thung lnga bcu rtsa drug rdzogs// g.yon gyi 'dab
8a5(1): gshog lnga bcu drug/ dman mo lnga bcu rtsa drug 'char// mdangs kyi thig le bcu gsum la// yul gyi ma mo bcu gsum 'char// dpal be'i thig sgro bco brgyad la// sems kyi ma chen bco brgyad gnas// mjug
8a6(1): sgrosgo'i thig le brgyad du shar// snang srid pho rgyud mo rgyud dang // ma mor grags pa thams cad kun/ khyung chen sku yi khyon du rdzogs// klu yi rgyal po nor 'dzin dang // srid pa'i bya khyung 'bar ba gnyis// gnod sbyin
8b1(1): bu mo rtag gdong mas// rgya mtsho chen po'i gting nas dkrugs/ kha rlangs nam mkha'i sprin du chags// klu dang byang chub sems 'khrugs nas// srid pa'i ma mo thugs 'khrugs te// de phyir skong zlog 'di ltar
8b2(1): ro// hUM/ ser mo 'od bzang mdangs bzang mo// mkha' lding nam mkha'i skar mda' can// 'di yi mdangs kyi thugs dam bskang // dkar mo 'od kyi zer 'phro ma// mthing nag 'bar bas thugs dam
8b3(1): bskang // dkar mo shel gyi mdangs bzang mo// tshul khrims rnam dag mdangs kyis bskang // gser bya nam mkha'i sprin dmar mgo/ mgrin bzang mo yi mdangs kyis bskang // dmar mo zangs kyi mig gcig
8b4(1): ma// ro 'dren kha 'bar mdangs kyis bskang // nag mo spyang gdong dbugs 'phrog ma// dran byed nag mo'i mdangs kyis bskang // me long ye shes kun gsal ma// sngon mo mdangs kyis thugs dam
8b5(1): bskang // mnyam nyid ye shes kun snyoms ma// gser mda' rig pa'i mdangs kyis bskang // so sor kun rtogs ma 'dres gsal// bsgrub bya dmar mo'i mdangs kyis bskang // bya ba nan tan mdzad pa
8b6(1): rdzogs// nI ra ti ljang mo'i mdangs kyis bskang // bag chags kun gsal dbyings nyid gsal// kro ta nag mo'i mdangs kyis bskang // snang srid longs spyod rgyan du shar// gzi chen dir ba'i mdangs kyis
9a1(1): bskang // nyon mongs gnas nas rig pa gsol/ khra ri khra mo'i mdangs kyis bskang // nyon mongs gnas nas rig pa gsal// skad cig gcig la stong gsum khyab// ro za nag mo'i mdangs kyis
9a2(1): bskang // dkar mo dpal chen yab la bzhad// ru tshe rkang ldan mdangs kyis bskang // nag mo kha 'bar stong gsum grags// srin mo dri za'i mdangs kyis bskang // dmar mo gzi mdangs 'od 'phro ma// zangs
9a3(1): sprin dmar mo'i mdangs kyis bskang // ser mo rlung zhon stong gsum khyab// rig byed gser bya'i mdangs kyis bskang // zhe sdang nad rnams byang bar mdzod// hUM thugs rje'i dbyings nas shar ba'i ma chen
9a4(1): rnams// rig pa gsal ba'i ma chen rgya mtsho ma// thugs rje rgyun gyis bdag la dgongs su gsol// nyi zla'i 'od kyis khams gsum gsal mdzad ma// byams mgon thugs rjes bdag la dgongs su
9a5(1): gsol// mi 'gyur dbyings nas shar ba gsang ba'i yum// gzung 'dzin spros pa'i mtshan ma gzhom du gsol// ye shes mkha' las kar tshogs rgyas pa'i yum// ma rig mun pa'i ling tog bsal du
9a6(1): gsol// 'khor ba'i rgyun gcod thugs rje'i dbyings nas gsal// las kyi mnar ba'i 'gro ba drang du gsol// 'dzum pa'i mdangs kyis dbang chen yab la sbyor// gzi mdangs bkrag la longs spyod mdzad pa
9b1(1): mo// yun ring dus nas 'gro ba'i don mdzad ma// chag nyams 'gal 'khrul ci mchis bzod par gsol// lcags sgong bco brgyad ru mtshon 'bar ba yis// nag mo'i rgyal mo blon mo la sogs dang // bar
9b2(1): mtshams blon mo kha blon gung blon mo// nyul byed go la la sogs blon mo'i tshogs// thugs dam chen mo dbyings su skong gyur cig/ srid pa mtsho bzhi las/ bya lung rgya mtsho nag mo'i mdos bskang bstan pa'i le'u
9b3(1): ste lnga pa'o// // phra men rgya mtshos yang gsol pa// ser mo'i bskang lugs gang lags pa// rdzogs sangs rgyas la bdag nyan 'tshal// rdzogs sangs rgyas kyis bka' stsal pa// yum chen chags pa'i lte ba
9b4(1): nas// bse sgong khra bo rdol ba nas// 'dam zan 'dab bzang yang rigs kyi mchu leb byung // ri rab chen po'i byang phyogs nas// shang shang te'u'i gzi mdangs can// lus ni gser gyi bum pa la// gshog pa
9b5(1): g.yu yi rdo rje ris// sder mo lcags sder rtse gsum 'bar// mgrin pa zangs kyi 'khor lo la// spyan ni 'bar ba me yi spyan// mchu ni zla gam 'bar ba las// lce ni rdo rje ha ru 'bar// dpral ba zla tshes 'bar ba
9b6(1): la// tshigs pa dung gi 'khor lo'i rgyud// tsit+ta rin chen 'bar ba ste// glo ba pad+ma'i rtse zur ldan// mkhal ma mu tig rdog ma las// gnye ma bdud kyi zhags pa 'khyil// mcher pa mchong gi mching bu sde// mgrin pa
10a1(1): dbang gi dkyil 'khor la// lte ba zhi pa'i dkyil 'khor 'bar// snying ga rgyas pa chen po ste// gzhug ma mngon spyod dregs pa sgrol// las bzhi'i yon tan kun la rdzogs// srid pa chags byed chen
10a2(1): mo la// 'di yi mdangs kyis thugs dam bskang // 'dod chags nad rnams byang bar mdzod// gser gyi bum pa g.yu chag can// cha snyoms ma yi thugs dam bskang // dung gi 'khor lo smin ris can// e ka tsa
10a3(1): ti'i thugs dam bskang // nam mkha'i 'khor lo mgrin rings 'bar// nam mkha'i rgyal mo'i thugs dam bskang // nag mo dung gi khol thag can// spyi phud ma yi thugs dam bskang / khra mo gzi mdangs chu gzhung
10a4(1): zhon// sring mo bzhi yi thugs dam bskang // rol pa dung gi mche ba can// dmag dpon bzhi yi thugs dam bskang // dkar dmar 'phyen ma sgra 'byin ma// gru 'degs bzhi yi thugs dam bskang // 'dam bya nag
10a5(1): mo gser mig ma// 'dod khams ne mtshan thugs dam bskang // sgrigs ma rgya mtsho'i rlabs la 'phyo// srin mo bdun gyi thugs dam bskang // dung gi spu ris gseng mchu can// shar gyi ma bdun thugs dam
10a6(1): bskang // ser mo 'phyo ba'i lding stabs can// lho yi ma bdun thugs dam bskang // dmar mo khrag gi mchu dreg can// nub kyi ma bdun thugs dam bskang // nyul byed sngon mo rlung la 'phyo// byang gi ma
10b1(1): bdun thugs dam bskang // nag mo gser mig bum pa'i lus// dus bzhi rgyal mo'i thugs dam bskang // bdud bya nag mo srin skad can// gdong mo bzhi yi thugs dam bskang // bse sgong lnga bcu rtsa drug
10b2(1): dang // dar ser ru mtshon 'bar ba yis// ser mo mdog bzang thugs dam bskang // hUM/ mi pham thugs rje dbyings las sprul pa mo// yon tan lhun rdzogs sku 'khrungs phyi bshol med// chags byed cha snyoms
10b3(1): kun la bzod par gsol// phrin las drag pos skye shi rtsad gcod ma// e ka dza ti'i sku la bzod par gsol// drag shul spyod pas khams gsum rdul du rlog/ srin mo bdun gyi tshogs la bzod par
10b4(1): gsol// thugs rje thabs kyis 'gro don mthar phyin ma// nam mkha'i rgyal mo'i sku la bzod par gsol// dur khrod bskal pa brgyad kyi gnas nyul ma// 'dod khams nag mo'i tshogs la bzod par
10b5(1): gsol// thugs rje'i rgyun gyis bring bring dgongs mdzad ma// las kyi srid mo'i tshogs la bzod par gsol// gling bzhi dmag dpon dri za'i 'khor skyong ma// dmag gi rgyal mo'i tshogs la bzod par
10b6(1): gsol// ri rab gling bzhi'i khams kyi 'khor skyong ma// gru 'degs chen mo'i sku la bzod par gsol// rnal 'byor kun gyi phrin las mthar phyin ma// dbang phyug rtsa brgyad tshogs la bzod par gsol// dus
11a1(1): gzhi dbyings nas rang bzhin 'char mdzad ma// rgyal mo bzhi yi tshogs la bzod par gsol// 'jig rten thog dang ser ba'i sna 'dren ma// gdong mo bzhi yi sku la bzod par gsol// bya lung rgya
11a2(1): mtsho las ser mo'i mdos skong bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // phra men rgya mtshos yang gsol pa// bzlog pa'i las rnams bshad du gsol// yang dag rdzogs pa'i don gsungs pa// bzlog pa la yang
11a3(1): gnyis yod de// ting 'dzin rtsal gyis bzlog pa dang // srid pa'i mdangs kyis bzlog pa'o// ting 'dzin rtsal la 'di lta ste// yul dang dngas ma rtsa gsum las// srid pa'i mdog gsum rang bzhin shar// dang
11a4(1): po lnga gnyis gsum du ldan// gnyis pa lnga gsum gsum par snang // gsum pa bcu tshan lnga dang drug/ bzhi pa bzhi nyid gar du 'phyo// nam mkha' tshangs pa'i bu ga nas// skar mda' 'bab pa'i tshul 'phros
11a5(1): pas// las kyi ba dan bskul byas nas// srid pa'i bskal pa 'od 'bar bas// rtsa yi mkha' 'gro 'od du 'bar// 'od zer lnga bcu drug tu 'gros// dwangs ma'i mkha' 'gro thig le 'bar// bco brgyad 'od kyi
11a6(1): zer 'phros pas// yul gyi mkha' 'gro gnas su thim// bcu gsum 'od zer mkha' la 'phros// phung po sgyu ma gnas su bsgral// pho brang gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du// dug gsum rtsa ba rtsad nas bcad// srid pa
11b1(1): mtsho bzhi las ting nge 'dzin gyi rtsal gyi bzlog thabs kyi le'u ste bdun pa'o// // mdangs kyi bzlog pa 'di lta ste// bsgral ba dang ni bzlog pa'o// bsgral ba la ni gsum yin te// 'khor lo gsum dang
11b2(1): bshags pa lnga// sbyor ba gsum gyi bdag nyid do// srin mo'i gzugs kyi ling+ga la// sgrom bu b+ha ga'i hom khung du// za 'og rkyal pa gser mig can// ltas ngan kun gyi ming bris la// de yi ske ru btags nas
11b3(1): ni// sro tsa na yi zag pas btags// 'bru sna lnga la byas pa'i gzugs// pu tra zla ba lon pa la// mgo bo bya yi mgo bo la// lus la ltas ngan spu yis brgyan// lag pa g.yas su 'gyog phur la// g.yon pa mchog
11b4(1): gi phur pa'o// rkang pa g.yas pa thog phur la// g.yon pa shing bu'i mchog phur ro// de yi lag tu gong ma gtad// de yi gnas lngar dgod pa ni// sa bon lnga ni dgod byas te// de yi steng du dgod bya ba// ral gri
11b5(1): sa bon lnga yis sbyangs// mar me lnga yis gnas lngar mtshon// stong pa lnga dang mnyes pa lnga// grub pa lnga yang de bzhin du// rtog pa lnga yang yang dag ldan// de ltar sbyangs nas bzlog par bya// hUM/ bdag nyid che
11b6(1): mchog he ru ka/ dbu ni nyi shu rtsa gcig la// phyag ni bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis la// sangs rgyas bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis bsnams// dur khrod rgyan gyis brgyan pa las/ khro tshul drug cu rtsa gcig sbrul// dbu la khyung chen
12a1(1): 'bar bas brgyan/ khyung gi ral pa sprug pa yis// yul gyi ma mo kun spyod de// nam mkha' spug nag 'thibs pa'i byad// dred mo ral 'dzin ltas ngan bzlog/ g.yas kyi gshog zur dang po
12a2(1): las// steng gi khro bcu 'bar ba shar// seng ge 'brug sngon 'thab pa'i byad// gnam lcags 'bar ba'i ltas ngan bzlog/ gshog zur 'bar ba gnyis pa nas// gsang ba'i khro bo bcu ru 'bar// glang chen rba la
12a3(1): mchongs pa'i byad// stag seng 'dzings pa'i ltas ngan bzlog/ gshog zur gsum pa'i 'od zer las// spyi dpal khro bcu 'bar bar shar// gnam la sprin dmar mched pa'i byad// bud med ral 'dzin ltas ngan
12a4(1): bzlog/ g.yas gyi gshog zung bzhi pa las// rdzogs pa chen po khro bcu 'bar// skar mda' sa la ltung ba'i byad// dbyig gi nor bu'i ltas ngan bzlog/ g.yas kyi gshog zur lnga pa las// ta kri ta khro bo bcu drug
12a5(1): byung // ri rab me chen 'bar ba'i byad// lci ba zas kyi ltas ngan bzlog/ g.yon gyi gshog zur dang po las// srog rtsa'i ma mo bdun du shar// rgya mtsho sbrul gdug langs pa'i byad// me tog bcud nyams ltas
12a6(1): ngan bzlog/ g.yon gyi gshog zur gnyis pa las// e ka drag mo spyan drug sbrul// mkha' la stag mo mchod pa'i byad// rdzi ba spyod pa'i ltas ngan bzlog/ g.yon gyi gshog zur gsum pa las// srin mo 'bar ma
12b1(1): bdun du sbrul// mkha' la bya rgod sder 'dzings byed// gter gyi bcud nyams ltas ngan bzlog/ g.yon gyi gshog zur bzhi pa las// srid mo bzhi dang rgyal mo shar// g.yu sha dkar mo rwa 'dzings dang // seng ge
12b2(1): dungu 'bod ltas ngan bzlog/ g.yon gyi gshog zur lnga pa las// nyi shu brgyad kyi sprul pa 'byung // rno dpal mtshon gyi ltas ngan dang // rma bya g.yeng ba'i ltas ngan bzlog/ g.yu sgong sngon mo yar ba dang // lcags kyi
12b3(1): ser ba thab tu 'bab// shel dkar snod du dug spyod dang // zangs sgong dmar po mthur du 'dril// mi bzad 'bar ba glad la bskor// nyi ma sprin gyis 'khrug pa dang // 'tshub ma dmar po'i rmis kyang snying
12b4(1): rtags dang // seng ge gangs kyi stongs nas lhung // shel gyi sgo nga yar ba dang // sprin chen ral pa'i rtags bstan pa// bong bu bcud chen zags pa dang // dbang mo nyi shu rtsa brgyad kyis// ltas ngan bcu gsum
12b5(1): slar la bzlog khyung gi mjug sgo brgyad po la// rgyal mo bzhi dang gdong mo bzhi// sprul pa 'od kyi phreng bar shar// bse sgong khro bo'i byad bstan te// lcug phran zor gyis 'debs pa dang // gza' skar 'khrug pa'i
12b6(1): byad byung ba// zor rgyan brgyad kyang rtse la skud pa chags// de yi ltas ngan slar la bzlog/ khro bo'i rgyal po khams gsum hUM sgra can// sku la zangs khrab dmar po'i 'od kyis mdzes// phyag na mdung dmar me lce
13a1(1): lams se lam// ba dan rtse gsum srid gsum g.yab mos 'debs// g.yas nas bskor bas srid gsum dbang du sdud// glad la bskor bas bdud dpung rdul du bzlog/ srog dbugs gzugs
13a2(1): la dbang zhing kun gyi drod la khyab// ltas ngan dmigs kyis bsgral ba'i dus la bab// de nas nyung dkar gyi rgyal pos brab la/ oM rak+Sha shrI he ru ka/ byi kram ha kram rbad/ de la du na rbad/ de nas bstab ste/ hUM/
13a3(1): 'jigs byed chen po zhal phyes shig khro bo 'bar ba'i zhal du bstab// ma mo chen mo zhal phyes shig/ dam can rgya mtsho'i zhal du bstab// pho nya chen mo zhal phyes shig/ mche gshog nu ma'i zhal du bstab// dge
13a4(1): bsnyen chen po zhal phyes shig/ ging chen tshogs kyi zhal du bstab// yas kyi bdud g.yos khA hi/ mas kyi sri langs khA hi/ srin po'i dmags tshogs khA hi/ sngags kyi a b+hi tsa ra khA hi/ bya bsad skyibs ngan khA hi/

13a6(1): spog cing 'phen// snying zan tsit+ta'i dkyil na gnas// shan pa 'bum gyi 'khor gyis bskor// srog zan chen mo'i dus la bab// sder mo khrag gi dreg pa can// gang la bya ba'i snying 'dren ma// rengs par khug la

13b2(1): bar du srin mo rkang btsug la bsgral/ hom khung nang du yu ba gzug za 'og sbud pas gan rkyal bstan// tsit+ta drung phyung lto bar gzhag/ tsit+ta pany+tsa lnga ru bya// rlangs pa nam mkha'i khams su 'khrigs// srid pa mtsho
13b3(1): bzhi las bya lung las kyi rgya mtsho las rdzas kyi bzlog thabs te le'u brgyad pa'o// // phra men rgya mtshos yang gsol pa// srid pa'i bskang lung ji ltar lags// rdzogs sangs rgyas la bdag nyan
13b4(1): 'tshal// yang dag rdzogs kyis bka' stsal pa// rtsa ba chen mo mdo 'grel dang // nyams na bskang ba'i rim pa'o// rtsa ba la ni 'di lta ste// rgyal po'i bka' rtags rjes su thob// de ni sku yi sa ma ya// bskyed
13b5(1): rdzogs sa bon rgyun mi gcad// 'di ni gsung gi sa ma ya// rig pa'i rtsal ni rdo rjer bsgom// 'di ni thugs kyi sa ma ya// rdzas chen gnas su sgrub pa ni// 'di ni yon tan sa ma ya// rtse gcig mkha' 'gro 'du
13b6(1): byed pa// 'di ni phrin las sa ma ya// sdom pa'i dam tshig rnam lnga pa'o// 'di ni yan lag sa ma ya// 'di ni sa gzhi rdo rje ste// 'das na phung byed sreg par 'gyur// ldan na yon tan gter du 'gyur// bskang na
14a1(1): gser dngul bzhu ba bzhin// srid pa'i bskang lung las rtsa ba chen po'i mdo 'grel gyi le'u ste dgu pa'o// // bskang ba'i rim pa 'di lta ste// rnal 'byor sdom la mi gnas pas// de tshe srid
14a2(1): pa'i ma mo 'khrug/ ma mo 'khrug pa'i byad bstan pa// yid du mi 'ong ya 'byung // de la gong gi bam gyis bskang // hUM/ nga ni ma mo kun gyi rje// nga ni rgyal ba kun gyi yab// nga ni srid gsum snying rje'i mchog/
14a3(1): yi bka' las ma 'da' zhig/ hUM// spyi gtsug g.yu yi rdo rje rtse dgu 'bar// g.yu yi ral pas stong gsum khebs// rigs lnga'i sangs rgyas dbu la rdzogs// bdag gi gang ba'i thig le las// bla na med pa'i
14a4(1): yab yum gnyis// pha ma med pa'i sngon du byung // sangs rgyas nyid pas shin tu bgres// 'di yi sems dang yul gyis skong // gnyis med sbyor ba'i 'od zer las// mkha' 'gro brtan 'bar sems ma'i

14b1(1): bskang // yum dang gnyis su med gyur cig/ phrag dog nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// gnyis med sbyor ba'i 'od zer las// mkha' 'gro gnyen gsal sems ma'i mchog/ mdzes pa chen mo'i dbu mnga'

15a1(1): les thugs dam bskang // rig pa'i yon tan rgyan mnga' ma// snang srid kun gyi b+ha ga'i dbyings// gcig pu kun tu khyab par mdzad// che ba'i nga rgyal bdag nyid ma// 'di yi dwangs mas thugs
15a2(1): dam bskang // rdo rje khros pas zhe sdang 'joms// rin chen khros pas nga rgyal 'joms// pad+ma khros pas 'dod chags 'joms// las mchog khros pas phrag dog 'joms// dkar mo ral gcig yab la

15b2(1): ma// za byed me za brag gyon ma// dbang po mdun gyi thugs dam bskang // mgyogs ma chen mo lha yi sring // khyung lding ma ni gshin rje'i sring // g.yag mgo ma ni klu yi sring // sder mo can ni gnod sprin
15b3(1): sring // 'phar rtsa bzhi yi thugs dam bskang // spyan gcig lha yi dmag dpon ma// ral gcig gshin rje dmag dpon ma// mchu 'jib klu yi dmag dpon ma// las mkhan gnod sbyin dmag dpon ma// nya sha
15b4(1): bzhi yis thugs dam bskang // dkar mo gzugs ldan mdangs mdzes ma// dmar mo me yi mdangs 'phrog ma// sngon mo ral cings glog bas mgyogs// dmar nag rus sbal chibs su bcibs// dmar mo
15b5(1): sbal pa nag po zhon// sngo bsangs sha ba chibs su bcibs// ser mo rlung la 'phyo zhing 'gro// ser skya 'phar ba lce brgyad zhon// rnam shes brgyad kyi mdangs 'phrog ma// 'di yi 'bras bus thugs dam
15b6(1): bskang // dung gi sbrang mo mgo mangs ma// lcags kyi spyang mo mche ba can// zangs kyi spyang mo lce mangs ma// gser gyi 'phang mo mdangs 'phrog ma// 'di yi rus pas thugs dam bskang // lha yi bu mo dung skyong
16a1(1): ma// gshin rje'i bu mo dri snoms ma// klu yi bu mo 'od 'phro ma// gnod sbyin bu mo shan pa mo// 'di yi sha yis thugs dam bskang // de ba'i bu mo lha mo dbang // dpal chen bu mo dpal mo
16a2(1): dbang // 'jog po'i bu mo klu mo dbang // gnod sbyin bu mo shan pa mo// 'di yi khrag gis thugs dam bskang // dpal chen thugs kyi bka' sdod ma// dkar mo zhi ba'i las byed ma// ser mo rgyas pa'i las byed
16a3(1): ma// dmar mo dbang gi las byed ma// ljang mo mngon spyod las byed ma// sgal tshigs 'di yis thugs dam bskang // zlog sgyur chen mo mdzad du gsol// dbang chen mo rnams bskangs pas na// dbang byed pho la
16a4(1): mi 'tshal lam// rdzogs sangs rgyas kyis bka' stsal pa// tshangs pa chen po mgo lnga pa// 'di yi klad pas thugs dam bskang // klad gzer nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// gnam ging dkar po mig gcig ma// 'di
16a5(1): yi mig gis thugs dam bskang // mig gi nad rnams zhi bar mdzod// brgya byin ser skya chen po la// 'di yi snying gis thugs dam bskang // snying nad thams cad zhi bar mdzod// lha chen b+hI gi ri ti la// 'di yi
